    <li> I&#x27;m really glad I bought this Emjoi Micro-Pedi. First, for the obvious reason, to remove calluses and make my feet pretty again. I&#x27;ve used pumice, those  long black emery file things, those \\&quot;cheese grater\\&quot; eggs, and got tired of all the stretching and bending and contorting you have to go through to reach all the areas you need to. I bought the Emjoi instead of the Amope for a couple of reasons. First, the reviews on the Emjoi convinced me the unit is a good one, and the price was better. Second, I like how the Emjoi&#x27;s sanding roller isn&#x27;t totally exposed, just on one side. That means the dry skin isn&#x27;t flying all over the place and you won&#x27;t find fine white skin dust on your ceiling fan if you don&#x27;t do it in a bathtub; can be easily directed towards a paper towel for easy gather-up and disposal.    I have zero problems with it being battery operated. So far, I&#x27;ve used it maybe 5 times and the sanding roller still has a lot of life left in it. It turns on and off easily; the roller comes out very easily for cleaning; the unit is small and can easily be held in one hand; it is easy to reach pretty much all areas of your feet and toes.     <li> I have deformed feet that require me to make appointments with a podiatrist for callous removal every three months.  I am now able to safely remove the callous at home, saving me a lot of time and money.  I am very, very pleased!</li>
